Most of the gsung-'bum is in the possession of Klu-sdings Mkhan-
po of Ngor.
Shakya'i bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis rang dang skal mayam
ched du nyer mkho sug bris byas pa mnams phyogs su bsdebs pa'i
tshan grangs gser mig 'dring (or: "drid) pa'i lcags kyu

KA
(de la glegs bam dang po KA rtags can la)
Dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi
ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter zhes bya ba'i thog
mar/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa rin po cher jug
pa'i sgor dang po mdo rtsa bar/ dge bsnyen nyid dang/ dge
tshul (f. 5v) nyid dang/ dge slong nyid dag gis snga ma bsnyen
par ma rdzogs par phyi ma mi bya'o zhes gsungs pa itar kun
gyi sngon du 'gro ba dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa thob pa'i brgyud
pa nas brtsams te/ gser chos gsung ngag rin po che'i chos
skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi bar sargga nyer gcig pa yan
chad la ldeb bu sum brgya zhe gsum yod do.

don 'dus zhes bya ba dang/

ngu don 'dus bcas/

SHRI
(glegs bam bcu gcig pa SHRĪ gyi rtags can la)
1. Kun mkhyen nyi ma'i gnyen gyi bka' lung gi dgongs don mam
par 'grel pa'i bstan bcos gangs can pa'i skad du 'gyur ro
tshal gyi chos sbyin rgyun mi 'chad pa'i ngo mtshar 'phrul
gyi phyi mo rdzogs ldan bskal pa'i bsod nams kyi sprin phung
rgyas par akrigs pa'i tshul las brtsams pa'i gtam ngo mtshar
chu gter 'phel ba'i zla ba gsar pa zhes bya ba la sdeb ma
Inga brgya dang gsum yod do/
/slar smras pa/
shākya'i sras kyi brtul zhugs (f. 24r) 'chang ba bdag/
/yi ge'i ma mo bslab sbyangs dpyis phyin nas/
yang mes bzo rig mkhas pa'i rgyun skyong phyir/
sku gsung thugs rten bris 'bur cha tshad bslab
Zde rjes phyi nang rig pa'i gzhung lugs kun/
7mkhyen cing 'doms la bsnyengs bral smra dbang chen/
Zkarma 'chi med zhabs pad gus bsnyen nas/
Zyig rigs sgra snyan sdeb sbyor mthar phyin bgyis/
Z og min gnyis pa e wam chos ldan du/
mkhas mchog mnams las zab dang rgya che ba'i/
legs gsungs bdud rtsi'i skal ba sbom byas nas/
skyabs mchog de dag mnyes pa'i zhabs 'gyur bsgrubs/
7gang tshe 'khor lo'i mgon mchog zhal snga nas/
khyod kyis gsar bsgrigs bstan bcos yod do cog/
ma 'ongs blo gsal rnams la phan ched du/
gyi nar ma bskyur phyogs bsdoms bsags dgos zhes/
/bka' lung lan gcig min par gtsug gi rgyan/
Zstsal bder (or: ba der) brten sngon chad a bang khrid lung/
7thob kun brgyud pa'i rkang grangs zhib bkral ba'i/
/pu sti gnyis dang gzhan yang don gnyer ngor
Zgang dag bris pa'i bstan bcos che phra kun
7par du bskrun na 'gro don che snyam nas/
zla bral bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chos rgyal che'il
7thugs rgyud bskul nas chos sbyin par gyi 'phruly
legs par 'grub pa'i glegs bam dbang phyug grangs/ how many
spel 'di rang nyid mkhas 'dod nga reyal dang/
7chen po'i sar 'khod khe grags mos blo yis/
ma yig gzhan phan sems kyis 'di bgyis so/
7tshul de'i dge bas nyi ma'i gnyen gyi bstan/
spyi dang bye brag brtse chen snying po'i zhabs/
Ze wam par grags zung gi ring lugs dag?
7sprin dus chu gter che ltar 'phyur bar smon/
/thub bstan gangs ri'i spo la rtag 'gyings nas/

- 25
/bcu phrag rig pa'i g.yu (f. 24v) ral rab rgyas shing/
/lung dang rigs pa'i mche rmon gzing ba can/
/'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i gdong lnga mngon mtho ba'i/
Zbstan'dzin mchog mams bskal brgyar zhabs brtan shog/
Zyangs pa'i nor'dzin dbang bsgyur mi'i dbang phyug/
chos rgyal sde dge dral lcam sras 'khor gyi/
Achab srid mnga' thang phun sum tshogs gyur nas/
/bstan 'gro yongs la dge legs 'phel gyur cig/
Abdag cag gnyen 'khor itos bcas byang chub par/
7dal 'byor rten thob dam pa'i chos dang mjal/
bar chad kun zhi legs pa'i yon tan tshogs/
Z'phel nas 'di phyi kun du dge gyur cig/
Z'chos skyob 'di mnams ji srid bskal pa'i bar/
chos min log rtog dri mas ma bs.lad par/
Zbstan dang bstan'dzin kun la phan bde'i gzhi/
'bad med gegs bral 'byung ba'i bkra shis shog/ /ces rang
dang skal mnyam ched du nyer mkho sug bris byas pa mnams phyogs
su bsdebs pa'i tshan grangs gser mig 'drid pa'i Icags kyo zhes
bya ba 'di'ang shākya'i bande tshul khrims rin chen nam ngag
gi dbang po 'jigs bral phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i lha
dbyangs can snyems pa'i lang tsho'i sde zhes bya bas sde dge
lhun grub steng gi rgyal khab tu bris pa dge legs rgya chen
po 'phel bar gyur cig/



Rgyud sde kun btus
/gnyis pa spyi bka bsdoms nas smos pa la'ang RDO RJE PHRENG
BA dang/ MI TRA BRGYA RTSA gnyis/
dang po slob dpon a bha yā ka ras rje btsun rdo rje mal
'byor mas byin gyis brlabs shing bka'i gnang ba stsal ba la
brten nas rgyud sde bzhi'i yi dam bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis kyi dkyil
'khor chen po bzhi bcu rtsa gyis phyogs gcig tu bstar ba'i bstan
bcos PHRENG BA SKOR GSUM dang/ de'i steng du darpa pa å tsa ryas
dge legs su byed pa'i akyil 'khor gsum bsnan pa'i bstan bcos kri
ya sa nutstsha (f. 96r) gnyis kyi dgongs pa thar rtse nam mkha'
dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i rdo rje phreng ba'i sgrub dkyil sbrags
ma rdor phreng mdzes rgyan gyi yig steng nas 'jam rdor la slob
ma sta gon dang/ kri ya'i phyag len bde mchog 'khor los sgyur
drug la sbyar te dkyii 'khor zhe lnga'i dbang bka' yongs rdzogs
so sor thob pa la/ thog mar
1. dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam dpal rdo rje lha bcu dgu pa
2. dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje lha so gnyis pa
3. mam snang sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i 'jam dpal rdo rje lha zhe gsum pa
4. gshin rje'i gshed dgra nag po lha bcu gsum ma ste PHA RGYUD KYI
DKYIL 'KHOR BZHI/
5. dpal dgyes pa rdo rje thod pa can zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug
pa lha dgu pa
6. thugs kye rdo rje zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha dgu pa
7. gsung kye rdo rje zhal geig phyag bzhi pa lha dgu pa
8. sku skye rdo rje zhal gcig phyag gyis pa lha dgu pa
9. gur mkha' 'gro lnga rigs bsdus pa lha nga gsum pa
10. bdag med lha mo nyer gsum ma
11. bdag med lha mo bco Inga ma
12. ku ru kulle lha bco Inga ma
13. rdo rje sgrol ma lha bcu gsum ma
14. dpal dges pa rdo rje mtshon cha can zhal brgyad phyag bcu
drug pa lha bcu bdun pa
15. thugs rdo rje zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha bcu bdun pa
16. gsung rdo rje zhal goig phyag bzhi pa lha bcu bdun pa
17. sku rdo rje zhal goig phyag gnyis pa lha bcu bdun pa
18. bde mchog rdo rje sems dpa' lha bcu bdun pa ste GNYIS MED
RGYUD KYI DKYIL 'KHOR BCU BZHI/
19. 'khor lo sdom pa lha drag cu rtsa gnyis pa
20. bde mchog sngon po lha re gnyis pa

98r) phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i thugs dam gyi lha mchog brgya

steng nas slob ma rjes 'dzin dang sta gon sngon du 'gro ba'i

inga pa

/rtsa ba'i bzhi pa bstan pa ring du gnas par bya ba'i slad

bgyis pa/ dgos ched rnam gzhag dang bcas pa'o/

bar ma chad du skye ba bzhes shing phags bod du bstan pa dang

ljongs su bsam bzhin skye ba bzhes nas sum ldan rdo rje 'dzin

Rgyud sde kun btus
grags pa de nyid gsan bsam sgom pa kun syi pha mthar son nas/
mkhas grub kyi go 'phang mthon po la mnga brnyes shing/ mdo
rgyud gang la'ang gzhan dring mi (f. 115r) 'jog pa'i mkhyen
rab kyis legs bshad kyi gsung rab mang du bskrun khyad par
rgyud sde'i phyogs la gshin rje rab 'byams dang/ bde mchog rab
'byams dang rjes gnang dang byin rlabs rig gtad sgom lung sogs
zur bka'i rigs phyogs su bsdebs pa sgrub thabs RIN CHEN "BYUNG
GNAS zhes bya ba 'di nyid bskrun
de nas ring mo zhig song ba rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i thog
ma tsam nas mkhas btsun grub pa'i khyu mchog THO YON BLA MA RIN
PO CHE LHA'I RIGS KYI BTSUN PÅ YE SHES DON GRUB BSTAN PA'I
RGYAL MTSHAN DPAL BZANG POS rgyud sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor zur
bka'i dbang rgyun gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir bzhugs so 'tshal
phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa'i bstan bcos NOR BU'I PHRENG BA zhes
bya ba mdzad del 'chad pa dang spel ba la sogs pas rgyal ba'i
bstan pa ring du gnas pa'i sman yon bla na med par gyur/
de ang dam pa 'di nyid sog yul du sa skyong zhang blon
drwa ma'i rigs shing sã la chen po lta bu'i brgyud du skye ba bźes
nas/ lugs gnyis kyis mngon par mtho ba'i mnga' thang 'gran pa'i
zla dang bral zhing/ gnam gyi lha 'jam dbyangs gong na chen po'i
lung las 'dzin cing/ chen po du ma'i zur phud la khrims kyi gser
shing lci bas gnod pa'i phrin las bskyangs/ de nas re zhig gi
tshe rgyal yum 'phags ma sgrol mas rab tu 'byung bar bakul bas
chab srid mchil ma'i thal ba bzhin du spangs nas/ ngur smrig gi
rgyal mtshan bzhes te bsil ldan gyi ljongs su zhabs sor bskyod
de ris su ma chad pa'i mkhas grub mang du bsten nas/ gangs can
du bzhugs so 'tshal gyi smin grol rgyab brten dang bcas pa yongs
su rdzogs pa gsan bsam mthar phyin par mdzad de/ de ang rang
nyid kyi gsung las/ dgu bcu nyer dgu'i lo yi snga rol nas/ (f.
115v)
/ma 'ongs 'byung 'gyur mi bslur gsal gzigs te/
7thar par bsgrod pa'i lam tshul ston mdzad pa/
rje btsun bdag gi ma la gsol ba 'debs/
shin tu mngon gyur me long 'char ba l'tar/
Zrnam dkar shel gyi 'khar ba la brten te
nub nas nub tu bsil ljongs nyul ba na/
legs pa'i dbugs dbyung mdzad la gsol ba 'debs/
skal idan skye bo thar par 'khrid rgyu dang/
bstan rgyun nor bu brgya rtsa brgyad ldan pa/
Zdrug dkar 8.yu yi phreng ba legs drangs pas/
bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel bar gsol ba 'debs/
Zrje btsun khyed kyi bka drin zla med pa/
Z'khrul med dran cing drin lan bsab pa'i phyir/
khyed kyi gdams ngag zhing 'dir ji mchis pa/
Zphyogs gcig bsgrigs pas 'gro phan rgyas par mdzod/ /ces
gsungs pa ltar rgyud sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor brgya rtsa brgyad kyi
dbang chog NOR BU'I PHRENG BA/ RJES GNANG ZUR BKA' BRGYA RISA/
SPYAN RAS GZIGS/ TSHE DPAG MED/ SGROL MA RNAMS KYI BE'U BUM
PHYOGS BSGRIGS/ BKA' GDAMS GCES BTUS sogs gsung rtsom mang du
mdzad nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa ches cher gsal bar mdzad pa
yin te/ skabs der bsdus pa'i dkyil chog NOR BŪ'I PHRENG BAr/

Rgyud sde kun btus
/mthong ba'i mod la byang chub sems bskyed (f. 117v) pa)
bzang stabs pus mo g.yon nas phyag 'tshal lo/
mdzes sdug yid dben panyta li ka'i mdog/
Z jam mnyen spu ring Inab lhub g.yo ba yi/
Zjigs bral 'phrog byed bde bar zhon gyur cing/
7 smra dbang gnas su bgrod na ci mi rung/ /ces dang/
nor buli pareng ba thog mar spel ba'i skabs/
/rnal 'byor rgyud kyi bdag 'jug yongs rdzogs pa/
shin tu gsal bar blangs pa'i skal ba bzang/
shin tu sngas par nam langs skya rengs shar/
skar la dmar mangs sngon skyes skra dkar gyis/
lag par shed ldan bukka srog rtsar bcas/
Akrom ka yang 'gul bzhin 'khyer ba ru/ kro ma
kha kha'i gtor 'bul nor phreng 'di gtad do/ /zhes dang/
/akyil 'khor spyi yi tshogs mchod las/.
nor phreng gtad pa bram gzugs la/ /zhes gsungs pas/
/byams mgon dang rje btsun 'jam dbyangs kyis mtshon pa'i rgyal
ba sras bcas kyis kyang gnang ba stsal nas byin gyis brlabs par
mngon la/ khyad par du dpal mgon zhing skyong bram ze'i gzugs
can gyis nor bu'i phreng ba gnyer kha mdzad nas phrin las rgya
cher spel ba'i grogs su zhal gyis bzhes pa yin no/
de'i rjes su ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i
gsan yig rgya mtsho ltar brant ti mkhas pa'i rigs las thar rtse
mkhan rin po che byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang pos blo dman gyis kyang lag tu blang bde ba'i dkyil chog
sogs phyogs bsgrigs kyi dgongs bstad mdzad pa'i dkar chag ni/
DBANG BRGYA NOR BU'I PHRENG MDZES kyi dkar chag dang brgyud rim
phan bde'i 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba bzhugs so/

Rgyud sde kun btus
/gdan sa og ma GTSANG RTSE GDONG ni/ bdag chen kun dga'
bsam grub sogs dus mchod bla brang gi gdung rabs mnams kyis
bskyangs/ khri chen bsod nams lhun grub sogs bstan'dzin dam pa
'ang mang du byon/ phyis su gdung rabs med kyang/ bar skabs skye
sprul rim byon dang/ deng sang sa skya nas zhal 'dzin gnang/
/gzhan yang dpal sa skya pa'i brgyud 'azin grags che ba 'ga'
zhig gi gdan sa la/ NGOR E WAM CHOS LDAN ni/ 'jam ngon sa skya
pandi ta chen po'i ye shes gzigs pa'i nor bu'i me long gtsang
mar (f. 37r) ji ltar shar ba bzhin
1. rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos agung lo zhe brgyad pa sa
bya lor btab/ de la rdo rje 'chang 'di nyid ni/ 'phags pa dge
ba'i rtsa ba yongs su 'dzin pa'i mdo las
de tshe jig rten mgon po'i sprul pa 'byung/
de tshe dge slong kun dga' bzang por sprul/
tshul khrims kyis kyang khyad par 'phags gyur la/
/thos pa mang zhing pha rol phyin pas 'phags/ /zhes sogs
dang/ mdo sde padma dkar po las/
kun dga' bzang po nga yi chos 'dzin pa/
Abde gshegs bye ba drug cu mchod byas nas/
ma 'ongs dus kyi tshe na rgyal bar 'gyur /zhes rdo rje'i
lung gis gsal bar bsngags pa bzhin 'od gsal 'khon gyi rigs su
'khrungs/ chung ngu nas dad brtson shes rab sogs rigs kyi, rtags
mams sad, shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ grub chen buddha
shri/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros soge las zab rgyas
kyi gdams pa rgya mtsho ita bu gsan/
mdo sngags rigs gnas dang bcas pa la thos bsam gyis sgro
'dogs bcad/ bsgoms pas nyams su blangs pas grub pa'i go 'phang
mthon por gshegs/ Tod gsal gyi snang bar rje btsun sa skya pa
yab sras sogs kyis rjes su bzung/ 'chad spel eyi phrin las kyis
rgyal ba'i bstun pa la ston pa gnyis pa'i bya ba mdzad/ sngags
phyogs gtso bor gyur pa'i gsung rab glegs bam bzhi bzhugs/ lhag
par rgyud sde bzhi'i smin grol syi gdams pa mkha' khyab tu spel
bas rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa la bka' drin mtshungs pa med pa'i
phyir rtsod pa'i dus kyi rdo rje 'chang zhes grags dkar gyi yi
ge phyogs kyi bu mo'i mna lung du bkod
mkhas shing dngos grub brnyes pa'i zhal slob kyang bsam
gyis mi khyab pa byon pas stod (f. 37v) mnga' ris nas smad rgya
mtshams yan chad du phrin las kyi rgyun skyong ba'i chos sde
che phra bgrang gis mi lang/ de ltar rdo rje 'chang nyid dgung
lo don lnga par grub mtha' snyogs nas gzugs sku'i bkod pa bsdus
pa'i rjes/ gdan sar 'khor lo sdom pa ngur smrig gar gyis rol pa
2. muschen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan bzhugs
te/ de'ang mus stag mo gling skyar zhong gi rigs su 'khrungs/
rong ston dang/ rdo rje 'chang sogs yong 'dzin bzhi bcu tsam bsten
nas thos bsam sgom gsum gyi pha rol du son/ rdo rje 'chang gshegs
rjes gdan sa lo gsum du mdzad cing/ gshegs rjes kyi bya ba dang/
chad spel rgyun bsrings (gsung 'bum pod gcig yod)/ zhal slob kyang
kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge sogs tshogs bshad dang/ bdag nyid
rdo rje 'chang sogs slobbshad kyi brgyud 'dzin mnams byon pas
tshogs slob thams cad kyi 'byung gnas kyang rje 'di nyid yin no/
/phyis mus bsam gtan phug tu thugs dam gong 'phel du mdzad cing
grub pa'i sar gshegs/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa gsum par gzugs
sku'i spros pa brtul/
seis 3. de nas rim par gtsang chu mig pa 'gar ston 'jam dbyangs
shes rab rgya mtsho ('jam dbyangs sa pan gyi rjes su bzung/ gsung
rab mang tsam bzhugs/)/
4. ngor chen gyi dbon grub chen birwa pa'i mam 'phrul rgyal
tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug/ (gsung 'bum pod gcig bzhugs)

Rgyud sde kun btus
gyis grub pa'i go 'phang mthon por gshegs pa sogs legs yon thams
cad bum nang gi mar me bzhin du sbas pa'i brtul zhugs 'dzin/

sdom pa gsum dang/ gsung ngag lam 'bras sogs rgyun gyi chos
sbyin dang/ khyad par sa ngor gyi zur bka' dang/ spyi bka'i dbang

sogs kyis brtse chen snying po'i ring lugs la bka' drin chen pos
khyab par mdzad/ skabs der sde dge chos rgyal chen pos spyan
drangs te zhabs pad shing rta'i kha lo bod chen po'i bsod nams
kyi mgron du snga phyi lan gnyis bsgyur te 'brel tshad don ldan
gyi phrin las bskyangs/ de'i rjes su



Rgyud sde kun btus
31. mkhyen rab mtha' yas pa'i mnga' bdag byams pa tshul khrims
lhun grub/ (dar rtse mdor 'khrungs)
32. brang ti mkhan chen grub pa'i dbang phyug byams pa nam
mkha' bsam 'grub/
33. rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi mnam 'phrul mkhan chen rdo rje
'chang dpal ldan chos skyong/ (ngor spel grong du 'khrungs)
34. mtshungs med mkhas shing grub pa 'jam ngon sangs rgyas
dpal bzang/
35. khang gsar ba mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams lhun grub/
36. shar chen byang chub sems dpa' rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal
mtshan/
37. mkhan chen bkra shis lhun grub sku dbon 'jam dbyangs chos
kyi bla ma sangs rgyas ye shes/
38. 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rje dkon mchog grags pa/
39. khang gear ba ngag dbang chos skyong bzang po/
40. mkhas grub sangs rgyas grags pa/
41. mtshungs med phun tshogs don grub/.
42. mkhas (f. 39r) grub chen po byams pa kun dga' bsod nams/
43. brang ti mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa byams pa nam
mkha' chi med/
44. rab 'byams shes bya kun gzigs mkhas grub ngag dbang dam
chos/
45. smra ba'i dbang phyug mkhan chen bsod nams dpal 'byor/
'di man chad rgyud sde sdud pa po'i chos 'brel thob pa'i mkhan
chen rnams kyi mnam thar cun zad bcas brjod par bya'o/
46. de'i rjes su byams pa kun dga' bstan'dzin ni/ brang ti
mkhas pa'i rigs su 'khrungs/ sku gzhon nu nas ngor thar rtser
phebs/ nam mkha' 'chi med las dom gsum nod/ kun tu dgos pa'i
gzhung bdun sogs thugs la bzung/ tshul khrims dris phyogs kun
tu khyab/ lhag pa'i iha du mas zhal gzigs/ 'od gsal phyag rgya
chen po'i gnas lugs mngon sum rtogs/ bod dang bod chen po'i ljongs
rnams su gsung ngag tshogs slob sogs chos 'khor rgya cher bskor/
kun mkhyen e wam pa'i bstan pa sri zhu chen po bsgrubs/ mthar 'pho
ba'i rnal 'byor gyis gzugs sku'i bkod pa dbyings su bsdus/
47. de'i rjes su khang gsar ba ngag dbang blo gros bzang
pos mkhan po mdzad/
48. de'i rjes su yongs 'dzin pandi ta dpal ldan chos kyi
rgyal mtshan ni/ shar mi nyag se'u rgyal po'i rigs las mgar thar
du 'khrungs/ sku chung ngu nas dam pa'i rigs sad/ dgung lo bco
brgyad par ngor du phebs/ ngag dbang dam chos las sdom gsum gyi
bkal drin nod/ kun tu dgos pa'i gzhung bdun sogs byang chub/ rje
btsun 'jam dpal dkar po'i rgya sran la brten nas shes rab kyi
klong brdol/ rig gnas che chung bcu tshegs med par thugs su bcud/
thub bstan rnam rgyal du rtsod grwar lo bdun bzhugs pas pod chen
lnga'i rab 'byams pa chen (f. 39v) por gyur/ sa skya bkras lhun
sogs su grwa skor mdzad pas mi nyag pandi ta zhes mtshan don dang
Idan par grags/ lha gdan smon lam chen por mandal ljags bshad dang/
pod chen lnga' i dam bca' bzhag/ 'bum dum pa bcu gnyis thugs thog
nas rgyug phul bas gzhung sa chen pos rgyal ba'i yongs "dzin gyi
cho lo dang/ gser mdog can/ skyed tshal og gzigs gsos su stsal/
rgyal dbang tshul khrims rgya mtshor tshe sgrub dang/ srid skyong
rta tshag la dbang/ sman rgyud bzhi'i bshad khrid phul/ ser 'bras
dga' gsum gyis rang gi bla ma bzhin du bkur/ ngor gyi mkhan po
lo bdun mdzad/ sras slobbskrun pa'i gtso bor ngor mkhan chen mnam
pa bzhi/ zhabs drung rnam pa lnga/ doon slob bzhi/ rig pa smra ba
gsum/ chos rje bdun/ sprul sku bcu/ bya btang ri khrod zin pa
brgyad sogs bsam gyis mi khyab/ gsung rab kyang mang tsam bzhugs/
dgung phrag nga gsum nas don gnyis par sgrub par rtse gcig tu
gzhol/ rje btsun sgrol ma'i zhal na ma 'dod du gzigs/ ikog gyur

Rgyud sde kun btus
thams cad phyag mthil du gzigs pa'i lung bstan dang/ yi dam las
chos gsan pa sogs grub pa'i mnam thar blo 'das su ston pas kun
gyis sangs rgyas su nges shes myed/ sku tshe'i 'du byed yang yang
byin gyis brlabs nas/ don gnyis par thugs dam grol mtshams/ zhugs
'bul tshul sogs dgongs rdzogs che phra thams cad bslab ston du
stsal nas sgras 'pho ba'i 'da' kha ma'i sgo nas sku'i bkod pa dbyins
su bsdus/ zhugs phul ba na me tog gi char babs shing/ dri bzang
pos gling thams cad zhag bdun la khyab/ gaung la a sogs rang byon
dang bcas pa kun gyis mchod pa'i (f. 40r) bsti gnas su thob bo
49. de'i rjes su phan khang mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong
gi sku dbon rin chen mchog grub kyi mam 'phrul byams pa dpal
ldan bzang po/
50. de'i rjes su brang ti'i mkhan chen byang chub sems dpa'
rigs brgya'i khyab bdag mal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po/
51. de'i rjes su khang gsar mkhan chen mtshungs med ngag
dbang blo gros bstan 'dzin/
52. de'i rjes su phan khang dbon rin chen chos mdzad kyi
mam 'phrul mkhan chen kun dga' bstan pa'i blo gros/
53. de'i rjes su brang ti'i mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa
byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi mnam thar ni rgyud
sde'i bka' bsdu'i shing rta'i srol 'byed yin pas 'og tu gsal/
54. de'i rjes su ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan ni/
snar thang dpal 'byor gling pa'i gdung rus las rong du 'khrungs/
sku chung ngu nay ngon khang gear du phebs/ rgyud chung bzhi sogs
bzung ba la thugs rab che/ kun dga' bstan pa'i blo gros las sdom
gsum nod/ byams pa kun dga' btsan pa'i rgyal mtshan bsten nas
phyi nang rig pa'i gzhung la mkhyen rab rgyas/ mkhan po lo bcur
mdzad skabs gsung ngag tshogs slob sogs chos 'khor rgya chen
bskor bas skal ldan gyi slob ma grangs med pa bskrun gsung 'bum
pusti gnyis tsam bzhugs/ sde dge chos rgyal chen pos mchod gnas
su edan drangs/ sa dgon rnams nyams geo mdzad pa sogs kyis bstan
la bka' drin che/ mthar kye rong khu phyag jo bo wa ti bzang po'i
spyan sngar sku mya ngan las 'das so/
55. 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho ni/ rigs kyi dbon dang/
mkhan ngag dbang blo gros bzang po'i rnam par 'khrul par rong du
bitams/ sku gzhon nu nay ngon khang gear đu phebs/ byams (f, 40v)
pa kun dga' bstan'dzin las sdom gsum nod/ nges byung dang snying
rje ngang gis 'khrungs, mkhyen rab kyi gter mdzod grol bas rgyud
chung bzhi/ phyi nang rig gnas sogs dka" ma med par mkhyen/ yongs
'dzin dam pa du ma las zab rgyas kyi gdams pa gsan/ dpal kye rdo
rje sogs lhag pa'i lha du ma'i bsnyen pa dang/ rgyun gyi nyams
bzhes rim gnyis zab mo'i rnal 'byor rtse gcig tu bsgoms pas lhan
cig skyes pa'i ye shes gzigs/ chen po gling gi rgyal pos ti shrir
spyan drangs pas 'brel tshad don ldan gyi phrin las bekyangs mkhan .
po lo bdun du mdzad skabs sdom pa gsum dang/ gsung ngag lam 'bras
sogs chos kyi 'khor lo skal ldan gyi gdul bya grangs med par bskor
bas smin grol la bkod/ mthar ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas
gzugs sku'i bkod pa dbyings su bsdus/
56. dpal ldan blo gros rgyal ntshan ni/ pad nag mdo rgan por
byams pa dpal ldan bzang po'i sku dbon du 'khrungs/ thog mar dga'
ba gdong gi chos grwar byon, jo bo bka' gdams pa'i ita spyod gdams
pa zab mos zhi dul lhod gsum gyi yon tan ngang gis 'phel7 de nas
ngor phan bde khang gear du phebs/ byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i
rgyal mtshan las sdom gsum gyi bka' drin nod/ gnang bkag gi bslab
gzhi spyan 'bras bzhin bsrungs shing/ bdag pas gzhan gces kyi
byang sems bdud rtsi'i rgyun gyis thugs kyi bum bzang yongs su
gtams/ skyes sbyangs mkhyen rab kyi padmo grol bas mdo sngags rig
gnas dang bcas pa'i glegs bam gcig pur gyur/ lhag pa'i lha rab
'byams kyi bsnyen pa dang/ chu bo'i rgyun gyi mnal 'byor (f. 41r)

'o
/gnyis pa brjod bya'i don lam gyi rim par bsgrig pa la gsum/
dbang bskur ba'i tshul/ dam tshig gi mam gzhag/ lam gyi ngo bo
/dang po (dbang bskur ba'i tshul) la gnyis/ dkyil 'khor gyi
rnam grangs/ dbang bskur ba'i tshul lo/
7dang po (akyil 'khor gyi rnam grangs) la bzhi/ rdul tshon/
ras bris/ bsam gtan/ lus akyil 1o/
/dang po (rdul tshon) ni/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas/
Zabang bskur dkyil 'khor sngon 'gro bar/
rdo rje 'chang gis gsungs pa ste/
Z' on kyang dkyil 'khor de'i rang bzhin/
Zci yin de ni 'di ltar bshad/
Zri mor bris pa'i las dang ni/
thig las tshon dbye'i rim pa dang/
Z'gro ba 'di dag rang bzhin gyis/
/grub pa'i dkyil 'khor gnyis med pa'o/ /zhes dbang bskur ba
la dkyil 'khor du gzhug pa sngon du 'gro dgos shing/ de la dkyil
'khor gyi bya ba sngon du gtong dgos pa'i thog mar rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor ni/ sa brtag pa/ sa balang ba sa sbyang ba/ sa
gzung ba/ sa bsrung zhing byin gyis brlab pa ste sa'i cho ga lnga
legs par byas/
de nas sa'i lha mo lhags par gnas te gnang ba gsol/ lha sta
gon gyi sgo nas dkyil 'khor 'bri bar 'gyur ba la byin gyis rlob
pa'i don du gsol ba btab nas snyan gsan dbab/ sta gon gyi dkyil
khor nam mkhar bteg nas/ ye thig ma btab pa'i gong du'am/ lha
sta gon zin pa'i de ma thag par bum pa sta gon tshul bzhin bya/
kun slong bcos pa la sogs pa'i tshes bcu bzhi tshang (f. 96r)
bas slob ma sta gon byed/ ye thig btab ste/ rdul tshon gyis dkyil
'khor lhag chad dang nor 'khrul med par bris nas/ phyag rgya gsum
gang yang ring ba dgod pa mnams sngon du gtang/ dngos gzhi dkyil
khor sgrub pa'i tshul iad bdag mdun tha dad du byed pa dang/
tha mi dad du byed pa'i lugs gnyis las/ grub chen dā ri ka pas
bde mchog la bdag mdun tha dad du mdzad pa dang/ dus 'khor la
tha dad du byed pa yod kyi/ gzhan 'phags yul gyi chen po dag gi
bzhed pa la bdag mdun tha mi dad du mdzad pa shin tu mang ngo/
/tha dad du byed pa'i lugs ni/ sngon bdag bskyed rdzogs par
bsgoms nas/ mdun bskyed sgrub pa la 'jug pa na/ rang nyid mdun
bskyed kyi' dkyil 'khor gyi dbus su phyin pa'i dmigs pa ang mi
byed/ mdun bskyed kyi gtso bo'i nga rgyal yang mi byed par mdun
bskyed sgrub par byed pa yin no/
/tha mi dad du byed pa labod kyi bla ma snga rabs pa dag
ni/ dang por bdag bskyed kyi mchod bstod bdud rtsi myong ba yan
sngon du gtang/ nyer bsdu mi byed par mdun bskyed la 'jug/ de'i
tshe bdag gtso bo'i nga rgyal mi dgos par mdun bskyed sgrub zin
pa na bdag bskyed kyi rten brten pa dang/ mdun bskyed kyi rten
brten pa bsre bar byed pa la bdag mdun bsre ba'i tha snyad mdzad/
de nas ye shes pa dgug gzhug dang/ srung 'khor kha sdom pa sogs
byed/ sta gon gyi dkyil 'khor las rang dra gnyis pa nyin re
zhing spyan drangs nas bstim/ de lta bu de la dkyii 'khor bdun
bsres su bya ba zhes bla ma'i man ngag zab par bzhed do/
/rgya gar ba'i lugs ni/ bdag bskyed zur du mi sgom par mdun
bskyed sgrub pa'i akyil 'khor gyi dbus su rang nyid (f. 96v) phyin.
par mos nas/ de nyid du bgegs bsang zhing sngags gnyis kyi don
begom pa nas 'byung bzhi'i dkyil 'khor srung 'khor gzhal yas khang/
brten pa lha dang bcas pa dkyus gcig tu begoms nas/ dbang bskur
rgyas gdab kyi 'og tu rang nyid gtso bo las mar me gcig las gnyis
chad kyi tshul du shar sgor bye nas mchod bstod dang bdag 'jug
len pa sogs byed pa dang/ yang bdag bskyed kyi mnal 'byor nyer
bsduli bar sngon du btang/ de nas mdun gyi dkyil 'khor gyi dbus
su rang nyid 'khod par mos te/ bgegs bsang ba nas bzung mdun bskyed

Rgyud sde kun btus
rdzogs par bsgoms nas/ rang nyid mdun bskyed kyi lha'i nga rgyal
byed pa'i lugs te gnyis su yod do/
1 /lugs gcig la sta gon gyi dkyil 'khor nub dang por spyan
drangs nas bsgoms pa'i dkyil 'khor la bstims pas nub phyi ma sogs
la spyan drang rgyu med cing/ spyir bdag mdun tha dad la 'jug
pa'ang tha dad pa dang/ bdag mdun tha mi dad la 'jug pa tha dad
pa dang/ bdag mdun 'jug pa gcig pa ste nu gsum gyis sgrub tshul
dam pas ma dag gi bzhed pa las byung la/ gang itar yang mdun
bskyed kyi mjug thog tu 'jig rten dang jig rten las 'das pa'i
lha la gtor ma dbul/ nang du khro bo bcu dang phyogs skyong sogs
dang/ phy roi đu'ang kho bo phyogs skyong bcu dang 'byung po
rnams la gtor mas tshim par byas/ nang du 'ongs te akyil 'khor
la bskor zhing sgo dbye me tog dbul ba sogs byas nas/ bdag nyid
'jug cing dbang rdzogs par blang/ slob ma'i don du gsol ba gdab
ste skal ba dang idan pa'i slob ma lhag gnas sngon du song ba
gcig (f. 97r) nas nyer inga'i bar zung du ma gyur pa dag la abang
bskur bar bya'o/
/gnyis pa ras bris kyi dkyil khor la brten nas sgrub pa'i
tshul ni/ sa phyogs byin gyis rlob pa dang/ bgegs bsrung ba sogs
kyi don dus gzung ba dang/ bsrung zhing byin gyis rlob pa ni
tshig ris cung zad bsgyur ba ma gtogs rdul tshon syi skabs ltar
bya dgos la) sa brtag bslang gnyis mi dgos shing/ sa lha dang
lha sta gon sogs ni byed dgos pa dang/ thig tshon gyi skor ma
gtogs pa rdul tshon gyi skabs bzhin dor len shes pa'i sgo nas
bsgrub par bya ba yin no/
/gsum pa bsan gtan gyi dkyil 'khor ni/ slob dpon ting nge
'dzin shin tu brtan pa dang/ slob ma dbang rnon khyad par can
la dmigs bsal du gsungs te bsgrub gzhi'i dkyil 'khor mdun gyi
nam mkhar dngos su sprul pa'am) mos pas bskyed pa yin no/
e bzhi pa lus dkyil ni/ rang gi lus kyi cha so so gzhal yas
khang gi rang bzhin dang/ rtsa khams mams lha'i rang bzhin du
bsgrubs nas/ phyi dkyil gang yang rung bar dbang mtshan nyid dang
idan pas smin pa'i slong ma la gzhung ltar abang sbyin pa'o/
/gnyis pa dbang bskur ba'i tshul la gnyis/ dkyil 'khor du
gzhug pa dang/ zhugs pa la dbang bskur ba o
dang po (akyil 'khor du gzhug pa) ni/ 'jug pa'i dus su
dam tshig dang sdom pa bzung nas 'jug dgos pas/ de la thun mong
ba byang sems dang/ thun mong ma yin pa sngags sdom rigs lnga'i
dam tshig rnams sngar med gsar du skye ba dang/ nyams pa sor chud
pa lam mtha' rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang bskur ba man chad dang
brel ba'i sgo nas rigs lnga'i sdom gzung lan (f. 97v) gsum du
bya dgos kyi/ mngon rtogs tsam begom pa dang/ rjes gnang tsam
gyis mi grub pas/ pan grub gong ma dag/ sdom gzung sta gon dngos
gzhi gnyis kar byed pa dang/ sta gon las dngos gzhir mi byed pa
dang/ dngos gzhi las sta gon gyi dus su mi byed pa ci rigs 'byung
ngo/
/sngags sdom skye ba nges par dbang bskur ba la ltos dgos
kyang/ dbang bskur rdzogs pa la mi ltos te/ dper na dge slong gi
sdom pa brjod pa gsum pa'i sum cha na skye ba bzhin yin pas/
sngags lam gyi gzhi rtsa sdom pa 'thob dod dang/ thob shes/
srung sems rnams nges par brda 'phrod pa zhig gal che'o/
/gnyis pa dbang bskur ba (zhugs pa la dbang bskur ba) la
bzhi las/ dang po bum pa'i dbang ni/ dbang gi bya ba slob dpon
gyis dngos su mdzad kyang/ skur byed dbang gi lha zur du spyan

pa'i lugs la) bshad rgyud rdor phreng las/ dbang bskur re re sa
re'o/ /zhes pa'i don bum dbang bcu gcig tu bshad pa sogs mi 'dra
ba mang du snang zhing/ de la ang thun mong ba slob ma'i dbang
dang/ thun min rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang gnyis las/
dang po la/ rig pa ye shes lnga'i nus pa 'jog byed yin pas
na rigs pa'i dbang ste/ me tog phreng ba'i dbang gis rigs gang
du nges pa dang/ chu dbang gis rigs der 'tshang rgya pa la gegs
byed kyi dri ma 'khrud pa dang/ cod pan gyi dbang gis (f. 98r)
rigs bdag gang gis byed pa rdo rje'i abang gis thugs mam par
mi rtog pa'i ye shes 'grub pal dril bu' i dbang gis chos sgo brgyad
khri bzhi stong ston pa'i gsung 'grub pa/ ming dbang gis sangs
rgyas kyi mtshan 'grub pa mnams kyi nus pa 'jog cing/ phung po
lnga gnas 'gyur/ nyon mongs pa lnga sbyong ba sogs so so'i dag
pa las shes par bya'o/
/rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang gis/ sku gsung thugs kyi rdo
rje gsum dbyer mi phyed pa'i rdo rje 'chang thob pa dang/ rdzogs
pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog pa dang/ khams gsum chos kyi
rgyal por dbang bskur bas/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi las thams cad la
dbang ba'i nus pa 'jog pa'o/ /'di mams la bum pa'i chu'i bya ba
rjes su 'gro bas na bum dbang zhes bya zhing/ lus kyi mi dge
ba gsum dang/ lus tha mal du 'dzin pa'i snang zhen gyi dri ma
sbyong/ bskyed pa'i rim pa bsgom pa la abang/ 'bras bu sprul sku
'grub pa'i nus pa bzhag pa'o/
/gnyis pa gsang ba'i dbang ni/ slob dpon dang las sam ye
shes kyi phyag rgya gang yang rung ba snyoms par zhugs pa'i
sangs rgyas thams cad zhu ba 'dus pa'i ngo bo khams dkar dmar
'dres pa la byang chub sems kyi dkyil 'khor zhes bshad pas) de
Ita bu'i bdud rtsi nyid yab yum gyi mtheb srin gyis blangs te/
slob ma'i khar bzhag pas bde stong gi ye shes khyad par can
skyes par mos pa des/ thun mong ba dag gi dri ma rdzun smra ba
sogs bzhi dang/ thun mong ma yin pa rlung sngags so sor snang
zhing zhen pa'i dri ma sbyong/ ngag gi rtsa ba rlung byin gyis
brlabs shing las su rung bar byas pas rdzogs rim gyi dben pa
gsum dang/ kun rdzob sgyu ma'i (f. 98v) rdzogs rim bdag byin
gyis rlob pa bsgom pa la dbang/ lam dus su dhū tir rlung zhugs gnas
thim gsum byas pa las stong pa bzhi skye ba dang/ deli stobs
kyis rlung sems tsam las grub pa'i sgyu ma'i sku grub nas longs
spyod rdzogs pa'i skur 'gyur ba'i nus pa 'jog pa'o/
/gsum pa shes rab ye shes kyi dbang ni/ mtshan nyid tshang
ba'i padma can sogs dngos kyi rig ma'am ye shes kyi phyag rgya
gang yang rung ba'i bha ga'i dkyil 'khor du rig ma dang 'du shes
gsum ldan gyis snyoms par zhugs pas dhū tir rlung rgyu ba la
brten nas khams zhu ba spyi bo nas mgrin snying ite gsang gi bar
du babs pas dga' ba bzhi skyes pas/ de dang stong pa nyid ro
gcig tu zhugs pa'i lhan skyes bde stong gi ye shes de nyid sher
dbang gi ngo bo ste/ des ni sbyang bya thun mong ba yid kyi dri
ma brnab sems sogs gsum dang/ thun mong ma yin pa gang snang bde
stong gi ngo bor 'char ba la gegs byed kyi dri ma sbyong/ de
char ba'i nus pa dang/ rim pa bzhi pa'i 'od gsal bsgom pa'i snod
rung du byas/ 'bras bu zhu bde lhan skyes chos sku 'grub pa'i
lag rjes 'jog pa yin no/
bzhi pa tshig dbang ni/ dngos su da lta skye ba med kyang
snod rung gis dbang bzhi par 'gyur ba ni dbang gsum pa mos pa
tshun chad kyis nges pa'i tshe na de nyid dper byas te/ des
mtshon pa'i zung jug gi go ba slob ma la brda sprad nas/ de la
go ba chags pa la tshig dbang thob par 'jog la/ de'i tshul ni/
bzhi pa de yang de bzhin te/ /zhes pas dbang gsum pa'i dus su

Terminatur:
/gnyis pa mtshan smos pa ni, rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu
ma'i brtag pa zhes bya ba brtag pa sum cu rtsa gnyis las phyung
ba/ brtag pa gnyis kyi bdag nyid kye'i rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma'i
drwa ba'i sdom pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rdzogs sol /zhes pa
ste/ kye rdo rje'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu ma ste seyu
'phrul rnal 'byor mas zhus pa'i brtag pa zhes bya ba/ rgyud rgyas
pa 'bum phrag inga pa brtag pa sum cu rtsa gnyis las phyi ma phyung
ba brtag pa gnyis kyi bdag nyia thabs dang shes rab gnyis su med
pa'i kye yi rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma sku gsum gyi bdag nyid tshogs
pa'am sgyu 'phrul gyi drwa ba sambha ra bde ba'i mchog yin pas
sdom pa rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po zhes bya'o/. /zhes so
/rgya gar gyi mkhan po ga ya dha ra dang/ age slong shākya ye
shes kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pelo/ /rgyud 'di ni pan



chen ga ya dha ra dang/ 'brog mi lo tsā ba shākya ye shes kyis

su bzhugs so/

MA RGYUD "KHOR LO BDE MCHOG
MA RGYUD las 'KHOR LO BDE MCHOG lal snga dar gyi skabs/
pan chen bi ma la mi tras rma rin chen mchog la bshad cing
dbang dang gdams pa gnang ba'i rgyun las bde mchog sangs rgyas
mnyam sbyor gyi srol byung zhing/ phyi dar la lo chen rin chen
bzang po dang 'gos lo sogs kyis bde mchog gi skor mang du bsgyur/
klog skya shes rab brtsegs kyis/ bal po pham thing pa mched gnyis
la bde mchog gi chos skor gsan nas/ mal lo sogs la gnang/ mal los
pham thing ba sogs mang no yang bsten nae gwan te ble mehog la
mkhas par gyur/ de la bla ma sa chen gyis gsan pa sogs nas bzung
sa skya pa la ches dar/ mar pa lo tsa bas na ro pa la gsan pa'i
rgyun las/ mar mi'i bka' brgyud la'ang dar bar snang zhing/ yang
mar pa do pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis/ nā ro'i slob ma ma na
ka shri sogs mang du bsten nas/ dbang dang rgyud bshad ma lus
pa gsan/ bde mchog gi chos skor mang du begyur/ slob ma'ang mang
du byung/ yang pham thing ba las pu rong lo chung dang gnyos lo
sogs kyis gsan pa'i rgyun yang byung/ jo bo rjes lo chen rin chen
bzang po dang rong pa 'gar dge sogs la gnang zhing/ phyis mas
g.yag sde ze dmar ba la brgyud de bshad srol (f. 177r) dar ba byung/
yang jo bo chen po las nag tsho lo tsa ba la brgyud pa'i srol
dpal spang sna ba'i rgyun du grags pa'ang byung ngo/
gzhan yang sum pa lo tsā ba dharma yon tan gyis/ pandi ta
dza ya se nabsten te mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i rgyud 'grel yan lag

rnams dang/ ngor lugs lha brgyad rjes gnang/ gur mgon khro bcu'i
rjes gnang bcas bzhugs so/
S 7gzhan yang gdams ngag la brten nas bkral ba'i smin grol GDAMS
gyi rgyun bzhugs pa/ rje btsun dam pa sangs rgyas kyi bka' srol NGAG
dam chos sdug bsngal zhi byed las thugs dam bde gshegs bcu gnyis
dang/ yab bka' 'khor lo bde mchog lha bcu gsum ma) yum bka' khros
ma nag mo rigs lnga rgyal chen bzhi dang bcas pa/
SHANGS PA BKA' BRGYUD kyi bka' srol las byon pa'i rgyud sde
Inga rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor dang/ 'khor lo bde mchog lha
Inga/ sgyu lus dbang mo che i dkyil 'khor mams bzhugs/
pan chen nå ro tā pas lho brag mar par stsal ba'i snyan
brgyud nor bu skor gsum las rgyas pa RAS CHUNG LUGS kyi bde mchog
lhan skyes yab bka' dang yum bka' gnyis/ 'bring po dwags po'am
ZUR MANG LUGS kyi bde mchog (f. 213V) yab bka' lha bcu pa dang/
yum bka' bcas/ bsdus pa NGAM RDZONG LUGS kyi bde mchog iha Inga
nang lus dkyil dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor bzhugs/
mnyam med jo bo chen pos bshes gnyen 'brom ston pa la lkog
chos su gdams pa/ ngog lo chen po dang/ shes rab rgyal mtshan nas
brgyud/ phu chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan la bka' babs/ des stabs
ka ba rin chen rgyal mtshan la gnang/ phyis snar thang pa gzhon
nu blo gros kyi bar du chig brgyud kho nar mdzad, de nas rgya
bkrol te rim par brgyud pa'i bka' gdams glegs bam rin po che las
byung ba'i THIG LE BCU DRUG gi dkyil 'khor bzhugs/
YE SHES KYI MGON PO PHYAG BZHI PA ni/ sngon gyi dus dga'
rab dbang phyug gis bstan pa bsnubs pa'i tshe/ gzhan gang gis
kyang 'dul bar ma nus pa la/ bcom idan 'das 'khor lo bde mchog
gis dbang phyug chen po'i sras su sprul nas bdud thams cad pham
par mdzad pa dang/ lo rgyus 'ga' zhig na mgon po 'di nyid dbang
phyug gi bur gyur pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'khor lo bde mchog gis btul
te dkyil 'khor du bcug nas dbang bskur bas/ me tog khra gdong ma
la phog pas gsang mtshan BYA ROG GDONG CAN du gsol bar yang grags
shing/ gang itar yang 'khor lo bde mchog gi rgyud mnams nas dngos
su bstan pa yin te/ bka' srung gi mchog tu syur/ mu stegs kyi
ston pa mkhol gyis na lendra'i pandi ta thams cad rtsod pas pham ma khol
par byas te/ bstan pa 'jigs la nye ba'i tshe/ chos skyong 'di la

Rgyud sde kun btus
95
gsol ba btab pas bya rog gi gzugs kyis phrin khyer nas/ slob
dpon arya de wa spyan (f. 214v) drangs nas mu stegs 'khor bcas
pham par mdzad pa Sogs ngo mtshar ba'i lo rgyus mang 'phags
pa klu sgrub yab sras kyis srung ma'i gtso bor mdzad/ rtsod dus
kyi thams cad mkhyen pa a bhā yā ka ra dang/ tsă mi sogs kyis
kyang thugs dam du mdzad cing/ dpal chen rgwa lo dang/ steng pa
lo tsā ba la sogs pas bod du spyan drangs te/ 'gro ba'i mgon po
phag mo gru pa dang/ zhang tshal pa sogs bka' brgyud kyi srung
ma khyad par can du gyur pa 'di la KAR LUGS dang/ ZUR MANG LUGS
kyi nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor gnyis tsam bzhugs pa yin no/
SPYAN RAS GZIGS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR
/bod gangs can pa'i pha chos rnying pa rgyal po bka' 'bum
las byung ba'i spyan ras gzigs 'GRO DUL GYI DKYIL KHOR ni/
rgyal po'i bka' chems kyi skor gter kha gsum du sbas pa/ grub
thob dngos grub/ mnga' bdag nyang/ ston pa shāk 'od gsum gyis
bton pa ma pi bka' 'bum du grags pa'i smin byed kyi dbang bka'
dang/ grol byed/ rgyab brten dang bcas pa'i rgyud ma nyams par
da lta'i bar bzhugs pa nyid do
dam chos sgrub pa'i bar chad sel zhing dngos grub mnam
gnyis bde blag ster ba'i rje btsun 'phags ma'i sgrub thabs kyi
bka' srol rgyud sde gong og so so dang 'brel ba mtha' yas pa
rnams kyi nang nas/ dir 'chi med grub pa'i rig 'dzin chen po
mam pa gsum gyi dgongs nyams gcig tu bsdus pa/ bla med ma rgyud
kun gyi bka' srol mthar thug pa/ snga 'gyur mying ma la bka
gter dag snang gsum du grags pa'i nang tshan zab mo dgongs pa'i
gter/ 'jigs bral gyi rdo rje slob dpon chen po 'od gsal sprul
pa'i rdo rje la rje btsun phags ma nyid kyis (f. 214v) mngon
sum byin gyis brlabs pa la brten nas klong chen dgongs pa'i
rtsal las zab mo'i gter rgya bkrol te skal ldan gdul bya mnams
kyi dpyid du mngon par snang bar mdzad pa 'chi med 'phags ma'i
snying thig gi dkyil 'khor bcas bzhugs so/

gi gus pas bgyis pa'o/

Brgya bzhi'i cho ga
Brgya bzhi'i cho ga legs mdzes 'phreng ba zhes bya ba bla ma ba
ri lo tsā nas brgyud pa bzhugs so.
ff. 43
By Sa-skya Gong-ma Kun-dga'-blo-gros annotating a text of Rmor-
chen Ngag-dbang-kun-dga'-lhun-grub
Margins: (r) Brgya -- bzhi
THE LEGEND
/na mo gu ru/
gang gi thugs rje nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis/
/tsa tur ru tra ming gi lhag mar mdzad/
/nyi ma'i gnyen gyur de la gus btud nas/
mchod sbyin brgya bzhi'i cho ga bshad kyis nyon) /de la 'dir
brgya bzhi'i cho ga la mdo lugs dang sngags lugs gnyis las/ 'dir
mdo lugs bla ma ba ri lo tsā nas brgyud pa 'di la don gnyis tel
gling bzhi (i. e. gleng gzhi) dang cho ga bya ba'i thabs gnyis so/
/dang po ni/ sngon lha'i dbang po brgya byin gdug pa'i nad
kyis (f. lv) zin pa dang/ lha rnams kyis zhus pal boom ldan 'das
kyi lha'i dbang po bdud kyis zin pa la dgongs nas brgya bzhi'i cho
ga 'di mdzad pas bdud bzhi las thar nas nad las grol te/ ming yang
brgya bzhi zhes btags nas rdo rje gdan gyi ka gdan gyi fog tu sbas
so/
de nas pandi ta lnga brgya'i nang nas slob doon tsandra gomi
zhes bya ba sgra la shin tu mkhas pa des bton nas dar bar mdzad del

ba la/ des rdo rje gdan pa chung ba la gnang ba'o/ (f. 2r)

rtse la/ mthe'u chung la lha'i bu'i bdud dkar po mdun du lha bshos
la g.yas med tog) srin lag la 'chi bdag gi bdud nag po mdun du mar
me la g.yas khram shing/ gung mo la phung po'i bdud ser (f. 2v) po

gnyer yod pa/ bzhi ka thor tshugs mig gnyis pa'i gzugs mams bzhag/

idan ting lo chang bu ste cha gsum gtor ma bsham mo/



Baud bzlog gi cho ga
Yum rgyas 'bring rnams kyi don bsdus pa shes rab snying po'i sgo nas
bdud bzlog gi cho ga bar chad kun sel zhes bya ba mdzes pa'i rgyan
bzhugs so.

ces mtshan gsol te 'jug bde bar blo gter dbang pos thar
rtse rdo rje 'claang gi dgongs bzhed Itar rgyud sde rab



Lambras slob bshad: Rgyud sde kun btus, Tsha
'byams kyi bka'i bsdu ba chen po bgyid skabs bris pa'i yi
ge pa ni rgyud gzhung la dad pa thob pa dge slong dharma
bha dras bgyis pa'o
('dis kyang bdag, sogs 'gro kun dpal dges pa rdo rje'i go
phang ia reg pa'i rgyur gyur cig/ /sarba dā kalya nam
bha wa tu/

kyi zhabs la dus thams cad du phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su
mchi'o

tu gsol/ /'dir dus gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi

ba'i chos la bshad nyan bya tshull sgrub pa mthar phyin nas

pa don gnyer rgyud la gus/ /gong ma'i dbang gis smin byas dam
tshig Idan/ /de yis nyams len rim pa gsal bar bris/ /rdo rje
'chang mtshungs bla ma rgyud pa yi//gsung las lhag pa cung

/bsdus pa dga' ba'i ngor byas (f. lv) gsal bar bod/

dhù ti pa bsod nams kyis sbyar ba 'dis sdug bsngal gyi rgya

shu bham/

Terminatur: /'di bzhin gyi tho tshe 'di/ lug 10 hor zla bzhi pa'i

Contents of the gsung 'bum of Mus-chen Sangs-rgyas-rin-chen according
to the Lha lung pa dkar chag:
/snyigs dus kyi rdo rje 'chang mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyi gsung
skor/ pusti gcig
1. Bstod tshogs dang gsol 'debs skor
2. Yongs dzin rnam thar (=3)
3. Lambras khrid yig dngos grub 'byung, gter kha skong bcas (=4)
4. Rtsa ltung 'khrul spong dka' gnad (=5)
5. Rdo rje'i rkyang mam bshad zin bris (=6)
6. Kye rdor rnam bshad snying po don gsal
7. Rtsa sngags kyi bshad pa'i zin bris
8. Bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub pa'i zin bris
9. Lū hi pa'i mngon rtogs gsal by ed (=7)
10. Nag po pa'i sgrub thabs
11. Lū hi pa'i zur 'debs
12. Bde mchog dkar po'i tshe sgrub
13. Gsang 'dus 'Phags lugs phyag len (=8)
14. 'Jam rdor sgrub akyil lhan thabs (39)
15. Sbyong rgyud akyil 'khor bcu gsum gyi dbang chog skor tshan gsum
16. 'Chi Tjoms dkyil chog
17. Tshe dpag lha dgu'i dbang chog
18. Tshe sgrub zhag bdun ma
19. Grub rgyal ma'i dbang chog
20. Sgrol dkar mngon rtogs dang, rjes gnang
21. Don zhags bsnyen sgrub (=10)
22. 'Jam dbyangs dmar ser rjes gnang
23. Phyag rdor U tsā rya'i rjes gnang
24. 'Byung 'dul rjes gnang
25. Mgon po'i rjes gnang
26. Mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang bya tshul
27. Dur bdag gi rjes gnang
28. Dud sol ma'i rjes gnang
29. Mgon po'i skor gyi man ngag 'ga' zhig
30. Gnas yig

lam zab thun mong ba dang/ thun mong ma yin pa 2/ bla ma rin 'byung/

sbyin rnams so so'i lung dang bcas pa thob/
bde mchog nag po pa'i rdul tshon gyi dal du dbang bskur ba/ lo
hi pa'i mngon rtogs chen mo'i bshad lung rnams kyang thob/
tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang/ 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dbang/ rjes
gnang la mgon po lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa/ lcam dral thun mong
ba/ mam rgyal gyi rjes gnang kyang thob/
good bskor 3 gyi khrid tshang mar thob/
lung la sa skya pa'i gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum tshang ma/ rje kun
dga' bzang po'i gsung 'bum/ rje sems dpa' chen po'i gsung 'bum/ 'jam
dpal mtshan brjod/ 'dul ba lung tshang ma/ spyod 'jug/ thugs rje chen
po'i bsgom lung/ sangs rgyas bsgom pa'i tshogs bshad/ (f. 4r) ma la

1. Tshad ma rigs pa'i gter gyi 'grel pa'i (rnam) par bshad pa rigs
pa ma lus pa la 'jug pa'i sgo bzhugs.
ff. 211 (ff. 1-221)
Terminatur: /de ltar tshad ma rig pa'i gter gyi rnam par bshad
pa rigs pa ma lus pa la 'jug pa'i sgo zhes bya ba 'di ni/ mkhyen
rabs kyi dbang phyug chos kyi rje dpal ldan sa skya pandi ta'i
gsung rab la shes nas dad pa thob pa bsod nams lhun grub legs
pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po de chos rje sa skya
pandi ta bltams nas lo sum brgya lon pa'i chu pho (stag) dge
byed kyi lo (1482) tha skar gyi zla ba'i dus bzang po yar ngo'i
bcu bzhi la thub bstan dar rgyas gling gi gtsug lag khang du
sbyar ba'o)...
(Buddhist logic; exegesis of Sa-skya Pandi-ta Kun-dga'-rgyal-
mtshan's Tshad ma rigs gter)

series.
